			health = 2

			e_iron_isles = { k_iron_isles = { de_jure_liege = PREV } }
			k_riverlands = { d_rosby = { de_jure_liege = PREV } }

	7996.1.1={
		add_trait="blackfyre"

			add_friend = 1317 #Орис Baratheon
			wealth = 150
			
			any_vassal = {	#Vanilla bug workaround
				remove_title = title_councilmember_king
				remove_title = title_councilmember_emperor
				remove_title = title_high_admiral
			}
			any_courtier = {
				remove_title = title_councilmember_king
				remove_title = title_councilmember_emperor

			}
			c_359 = { #Квентон Qoherys
				remove_all_job_titles = yes		
				give_job_title = job_marshal
			}
		}	
	}
	7996.1.1 = { #Bleeding Years
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { year = 7998 }

			}	
		}
	}
	7998.1.1 = {
		effect = {	
			set_global_flag = aegons_conquest
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { year = 7999 } 
					NOT = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ai = no }
					character_event = { id = aegons_landing.1 } 
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { ai = yes }
					character_event = { id = aegons_landing.1 days = 1 } 
				}
				b_stone_drum = { ROOT = { capital = PREV } }
			}
			c_1317 = {	#Орис Baratheon
				remove_all_job_titles = yes

				#give_minor_title = title_hand_of_the_king
			}	
			c_38052 = {	#Деймон Velaryon
				remove_all_job_titles = yes	
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Zeus" }
					give_minor_title = title_high_admiral
				}	
				else = {
					give_minor_title = title_high_admiral_B
				}
			}
			c_3000050 = {	#Криспиан Celtigar
				remove_all_job_titles = yes

	}
	8103.1.1={ #becomes Деймон's lover
		effect = {
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = {
					random_dynasty_member = {
						limit = { character = 779496 }
						add_friend = ROOT
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { year = 8120 } }
							add_lover = ROOT
							if = {
								limit = { is_ruler = yes }
								ROOT = { 
									move_character = PREV 
								}
								add_consort = ROOT
							}
							if = {
								limit = { 
									is_ruler = no 
									NOT = { year = 8105 }
								}
								liege = {
									ROOT = { 
										move_character = PREV 
									}
								}	
							}
						}	
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.8.1 } }	# Accepted Эйгон's offer

				set_character_flag = against_king
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	8129.8.1={
		effect = {
			prisoner = no
		}
	}
